 fokas sirf gend, khilaadi or goalpost par he

 modern hockey main fitaness ko team kii kamyaabi kaa mantra mana jaataa he

 coach kehete hai ki unhen team kaa andaaza he or team ko unke bare main maaloom he
 So it cannot be said that they are starting from zero
 coach oltmens ko kamyaabi kaa fan maaloom he
 They take care of every nuance of the team and the player
 maidan par ek general kii bhoomika main hote hai to maidan ke baahar khilaadiyon ke khan-paan se lekar neend tak kaa puraa khyaal rakhte hai
 The players are beginning to understand why and what the coaches expect from them in the camp
 team hockey india ne beete ek saal main kai aisi kamyaabi hasil kii jisane hockey fans main badi ummid jagaai
 Defeating Pakistan in the final of the Incheon Asiad or defeating a team like Holland in the Champions Trophy in Bhubaneswar gave wings to the team's morale
 isi hausale ke sahare is team ne ajalan shah cap main australia jaisi team ko shikast de di
 Despite almost half a dozen players not fully fit in the World Hockey League semi-finals held in Belgium, the team stood fourth after Australia, Belgium and Britain
 lekin hockey ke adhikariyon ne is kamyaabi ko carat main badalane main der nahin lagaai
 It is another matter that players and coaches started talking about recovering from this loss as fast as possible
 1980 ke aakhri olympic medal ko hasil kiye 35 saal biit gaye hai
 Since then, the wait for the Olympic medal has been increasing
 shahrukh kii chak de parde par chaahe jitani hit rahi he bhartiya team ke liye sahi myne main chak de kehane kii chunauti barqaraar he
 The Olympic rate Olympics These teams keep increasing
 maujuuda team ek ummid jagaati he
 If the experts praise the merits of the team, then there is also a hint of deficiencies
 coach oltmens ne team hockey india kii penlti corner ko lekar bhi chintaa jataai he
 Indian drag flickers are considered great, but it is important to know how much they have compared to other countries of the world
 england ke eshle jackson, australia ke Chris Ciriello or germany ke philip jailer duniya ke maahir draig filkars maane jate hai
 The team as strong as drag flickers
 
 
 wo team utani hi kaamyaab! landan olympix se abtak bharat ne abtak top das tiimon ke kilaaf 67 maichon main 120 gol kiye or 176 gol khaaye! in 120 gol main 34 gol penlti corner ke zariye aaye
 India scored 24 penalty corners during the Champions Trophy and World Hockey League tournaments, in which the team scored just 9 goals
 jabaki bharat ke kilaaf inhen toornament main 41 penlti corner bane jinamein 14 gol hue
 Creating a penalty corner and turning it into a goal has proved to be a weak link for Team India in the recent tournament
 is ek kami ko dur kar bhartiya team bade kitaab jeet sakati he
 Experts say that the Indian team has power in the battery of short corner specialist but coaches Altmans are looking for other specialist besides Raghunath and Bob ie Rupinder
 gurjindar or jasjit jaise khilaadi achche vikalp ke taur par ubhar rahe hai
 Rupinder and VR Raghunath believe that the direction of their practice is right and they are expecting a lot from themselves and the team
 alag setapis, alag combination kii talash kii ja rahi he taaki bade maichon main iskaa bada faaydaa utaya ja sake
 Forward players are being told the tricks of penalty corner technique
 tippaniyan The team can definitely get the benefit of high altitude training at Shilaru at an altitude of 8000 ft above sea level
 lekin olympic ke podium kii oonchai tak pahunchane se pehle team kii chunautiyaan behad bad gai hai jiskaa jawaab puure hockey tantra ko dhundhna padegaa
 It can be said that no matter what the situation outside the field
 
 
 maidan par team kaa utsaah badhane laga he
 No lack of passion
 fokas pich par he or nazren podium par
 Gurbaz is the star midfielder of the team and the captain and coach understand his importance well
 sardaar kehete hai ki gurbaj team ke behad ahm khilaadi hai lekin wo maanate hai ki team sabase upar he
 Coach Altmans says that this issue is more about understanding and knowledge than indiscipline in the team
 shilaru main team kaa yo-yo test bhi kiya gaya
 One of the most senior players of the team, Gurbaj Singh topped it, one of the youngest players of the team, Aamir Khan was second
 senior or junior khilaadiyon ke bich kaa ye faaslaa shaayad team kii sabase badi taaqat he
 That is, 26-year-old Gurbaz and 22-year-old Aamir Khan are as fit as the top teams in the world, Australia, Holland or Germany
 lekin team ke australian fitaness trainer mathew iles (mat) abhi isse santusht nahin
 At Shilaru's high altitude training camp, he keeps on encouraging the players to get beyond their limits
 wo maanate hai ki team ke kai khilaadi behad fit hai
 They praise the fitness of players like Dharmaveer, Kothajit, Chinglensana, Gurbaj
 lekin unka kahana he ki isamen or bhi sudhaar kii ganjaish he
 Matt knows that in order to keep the enthusiasm of the players, he will also have to compete with them
 isliye practice ke baad coach tushaar khandekar ke saath res main khud ko aazamaa rahe hai
 But in the race, the game gets beaten
 vaise bhi tushaar ne haal hi main khilaadi se coach banane kaa safar tay kiya he isliye unki fitaness kaa level thodaa behatar he
 Speed determines the ability of a hockey team
 aise kai vaakye hai jab bhartiya team aakiri lamhon main match ganvaati nazar ai he
 Today is the test of the speed of the players
 speed get naam ke yantra ke sahare yahaan khilaadiyon kaa speed test ho rahaa he
 The players are in form and in a race to beat each other
 team ke shandaar forward esavi sunil, srijesh or lalit jaise khilaadiyon se baazi markar awwal number par rahete hai
 During the match, Sunil has been creating fear in opposition teams many times with the help of his speed
 hockey team or vivaad ek duusare ke peeche saaye kii tarah lage rahe hai
 This has not affected the health of the team, it can only be considered as an officially released statement
 team kii shaareerik or maansik sehat ko thik karne kii zimmedaari team ke saport staff par pehle se zyaada bad gai he
 Dutch coach Rolant Altmans is considered a highly skilled coach
 unhen holland team ko olympix, world cap or champions trophy main kamyaabi hasil karwaane kaa gaurav hasil he
 He has been associated with the Indian team as a high performance director for the last three years
 lekin team hockey india ke coach kii zimmedaari un par achaanak aan padi he1 acchhee baat ye he ki coach or khilaadiyon ne is badlaav ko sakaaratmak taur par liya he
 The coach says that he has an idea of the team and the team knows about him
 isliye ye nahin kaha ja saktaa ki wo zero se shuruyaat kar rahe hai
 Coach Altmans knows the fun of success
 wo team or khilaadi kii har baarik baat kaa khyaal rakhte hai
 When they are in the role of a general on the field, they take full care of the players from the food to the outside of the field
 khilaadi samajhane lage hai ki coach camp main unase kyon or kya ummiden rakhte hai
 Team Hockey India achieved many such successes in the last one year which raised great hope in Hockey Fans
 inchiyan asiad ke final main pakistan ko haraana yaa phir bhubaneshwar main hui champions trophy main holland jaisi team ko shikast dene se team ke hausalon ko pankh lag gaye
 With this encouragement, this team defeated a team like Australia in Azlan Shah Cup
 belgium main hui world hockey lig semifinal main qareeb aadhe darjan khilaadiyon ke puri tarah se fit nahin hone ke baavjood ye team australia, belgium or britain ke baad chauthe number par rahi
 But hockey officials did not take long to convert this success into a carat
 ye or baat he ki khilaadi or coach utani hi tezi se is nuksaan se ubarne kii baat karne lage
 35 years have passed since the last Olympic medal was won in 1980
 tab se lekar abtak olympic medal ko lekar intazaar badhata ja rahaa he
 Shahrukh's Chak De is as much a hit on screen as it is a challenge for the Indian team to truly say Chak De
 olympix dar olympix ye tis badhati hi jaati he
 The current team raises an expectation
 jaankaar team kii khoobiyon kii taareef karte hai to kamiyon kii ore ishaara bhi miltaa rahaa he
 Coach Altmans has also raised concerns about Team Hockey India's penalty corner
 bhartiya draig flikars umdaa to maane jate hai, lekin duniya ke duusare deshon kii tulana main unamem kitna dam he ye jaananaa zaruri he
 Ashley Jackson of England, Chris Ciriello of Australia and Philip Zeller of Germany are considered the world's leading drag filmmakers
 jis team ke draig flikars jitne damdaar
 
 
 That team was equally successful! India has scored 120 goals and scored 176 goals in 67 matches against the top ten teams from London Olympics so far! Of these 120 goals, 34 goals came through penalty corners
 bharat ne champions trophy or world hockey lig toornament ke dauraan 24 penlti corner ke mauqe banaaye jinamein is team ne sirf 9 gol kiye
 While 41 penalty corners were scored in these tournament against India in which 14 goals were scored
 penlti corner bananaa or use gol main tabdeel karnaa haal ke toornament main team india kii kamazor kadi sabit hui he
 By removing this one deficiency, the Indian team can win a big title
 jaankaar kehete hai ki bhartiya team kii short corner specialist kii bydaree main dam to he lekin coach oltmens raghunatha or bob yani rupinder ke alaava bhi duusare specialist kii talash main hai
 Players like Gurjinder and Jasjeet are emerging as good options
 rupinder or viaar raghunatha maanate hai ki unki abhyaas kii disha sahi he or wo khud se or team se badi ummid rakh rahe hai
 Separate setpieces, separate combinations are being looked for so that it can be exploited in big matches
 forward khilaadiyon ko penlti corner banane kii takanic ke gur bataaye ja rahe hai
 The comments samudr tal se 8000 fit kii oonchai par shilaru main hai oltitude training kaa kaa faaydaa team ko zarur mil saktaa he
 But before the Olympics reach the height of the podium, the team's challenges have increased immensely, the answer will be to find the entire hockey system
 itnaa zarur kaha ja saktaa he ki maidan ke baahar halaat chaahe jaise bhi hon

 josh kii kami nahin
 Focus is on the pitch and eyes on the podium

 yani 26 saal ke gurbaj or 22 saal ke aamir khan utane hi fit hai jitna ki duniya kii top team australia, holland yaa germany ke khilaadi hai
 But the team's Australian fitness trainer Matthew Isles (matt) is not satisfied yet
 shilaru ke hai oltitude training camp main wo khilaadiyon ko unki had se aage nikalne ke liye josh bharte rahete hai
 He believes that many of the team's players are very fit
 wo dharmaveer, kothajit, chingalensana, gurbaj jaise khilaadiyon ke naam lekar inaki fitaness kii taareef karte hai
 But he says that there is scope for further improvement
 mat jaanate hai ki khilaadiyon kaa utsaah banaaye rakhane ke liye unhen khud bhi unase compit karnaa hoga
 Therefore, after practice, the coach is trying himself in the race with Tusshar Khandekar
 lekin res main tushaar baazi maar jate hai
 Anyway, Tushar has recently decided to go from player to coach, so his fitness level is slightly better
 speed, hockey team kii kaabiliyat tay karti he
 There have been many instances when the Indian team has been seen losing matches in the last moments
 aaj khilaadiyon kii raftaar kaa imtihaan he
 The speed test of the players is being done here with the help of a device called Speed gate
 khilaadi form main hai or ek duusare ko pachhaadne kii hode main bhi
 The team's great forwards, SV Sunil, Sreejesh and Lalit are ranked number one by beating players
 match ke dauraan apni speed ke sahare sunil kai baar vipakshi tiimon main khof paidaa karte rahe hai
 The hockey team and the controversy are behind each other like shadows
 iskaa asar team kii sehat par kuch bhi naa padaa ho ise sirf aadhikarik taur jari bayaan hi mana ja saktaa he
 The responsibility of recovering the physical and mental health of the team has increased more than ever on the support staff of the team
 dach coach rolent oltmens behad maahir coach maane jate hai

 alag setapis, alag combination kii talash kii ja rahi he taaki bade maichon main iskaa bada faaydaa utaya ja sake
 Forward players are being told the tricks of penalty corner technique
 tippaniyan The team can definitely get the benefit of high altitude training at Shilaru at an altitude of 8000 ft above sea level
 lekin olympic ke podium kii oonchai tak pahunchane se pehle team kii chunautiyaan behad bad gai hai jiskaa jawaab puure hockey tantra ko dhundhna padegaa

 maidan par team kaa utsaah badhane laga he
 No lack of passion
 fokas pich par he or nazren podium par

 But in the race, the game gets beaten
 vaise bhi tushaar ne haal hi main khilaadi se coach banane kaa safar tay kiya he isliye unki fitaness kaa level thodaa behatar he
 Speed determines the ability of a hockey team
 aise kai vaakye hai jab bhartiya team aakiri lamhon main match ganvaati nazar ai he
 Today is the test of the speed of the players
 speed get naam ke yantra ke sahare yahaan khilaadiyon kaa speed test ho rahaa he
 The players are in form and in a race to beat each other
 team ke shandaar forward esavi sunil, srijesh or lalit jaise khilaadiyon se baazi markar awwal number par rahete hai
 During the match, Sunil has been creating fear in opposition teams many times with the help of his speed
 hockey team or vivaad ek duusare ke peeche saaye kii tarah lage rahe hai
 This has not affected the health of the team, it can only be considered as an officially released statement
 team kii shaareerik or maansik sehat ko thik karne kii zimmedaari team ke saport staff par pehle se zyaada bad gai he
 Dutch coach Rolant Altmans is considered a highly skilled coach
 unhen holland team ko olympix, world cap or champions trophy main kamyaabi hasil karwaane kaa gaurav hasil he
 He has been associated with the Indian team as a high performance director for the last three years
 lekin team hockey india ke coach kii zimmedaari un par achaanak aan padi he1 acchhee baat ye he ki coach or khilaadiyon ne is badlaav ko sakaaratmak taur par liya he

 isliye ye nahin kaha ja saktaa ki wo zero se shuruyaat kar rahe hai

 wo team or khilaadi kii har baarik baat kaa khyaal rakhte hai

 Team Hockey India achieved many such successes in the last one year which raised great hope in Hockey Fans
 inchiyan asiad ke final main pakistan ko haraana yaa phir bhubaneshwar main hui champions trophy main holland jaisi team ko shikast dene se team ke hausalon ko pankh lag gaye
 With this encouragement, this team defeated a team like Australia in Azlan Shah Cup
 belgium main hui world hockey lig semifinal main qareeb aadhe darjan khilaadiyon ke puri tarah se fit nahin hone ke baavjood ye team australia, belgium or britain ke baad chauthe number par rahi
 But hockey officials did not take long to convert this success into a carat
 ye or baat he ki khilaadi or coach utani hi tezi se is nuksaan se ubarne kii baat karne lage

 tab se lekar abtak olympic medal ko lekar intazaar badhata ja rahaa he

 olympix dar olympix ye tis badhati hi jaati he

 bhartiya draig flikars umdaa to maane jate hai, lekin duniya ke duusare deshon kii tulana main unamem kitna dam he ye jaananaa zaruri he
 Ashley Jackson of England, Chris Ciriello of Australia and Philip Zeller of Germany are considered the world's leading drag filmmakers
 jis team ke draig flikars jitne damdaar
 
 
 That team was equally successful! India has scored 120 goals and scored 176 goals in 67 matches against the top ten teams from London Olympics so far! Of these 120 goals, 34 goals came through penalty corners
 bharat ne champions trophy or world hockey lig toornament ke dauraan 24 penlti corner ke mauqe banaaye jinamein is team ne sirf 9 gol kiye
 While 41 penalty corners were scored in these tournament against India in which 14 goals were scored
 penlti corner bananaa or use gol main tabdeel karnaa haal ke toornament main team india kii kamazor kadi sabit hui he
 By removing this one deficiency, the Indian team can win a big title
 jaankaar kehete hai ki bhartiya team kii short corner specialist kii bydaree main dam to he lekin coach oltmens raghunatha or bob yani rupinder ke alaava bhi duusare specialist kii talash main hai
 Players like Gurjinder and Jasjeet are emerging as good options
 rupinder or viaar raghunatha maanate hai ki unki abhyaas kii disha sahi he or wo khud se or team se badi ummid rakh rahe hai
 Separate setpieces, separate combinations are being looked for so that it can be exploited in big matches
 forward khilaadiyon ko penlti corner banane kii takanic ke gur bataaye ja rahe hai

 Separate setpieces, separate combinations are being looked for so that it can be exploited in big matches
 forward khilaadiyon ko penlti corner banane kii takanic ke gur bataaye ja rahe hai
 The comments samudr tal se 8000 fit kii oonchai par shilaru main hai oltitude training kaa kaa faaydaa team ko zarur mil saktaa he
 But before the Olympics reach the height of the podium, the team's challenges have increased immensely, the answer will be to find the entire hockey system
 itnaa zarur kaha ja saktaa he ki maidan ke baahar halaat chaahe jaise bhi hon
 
 
 The enthusiasm of the team on the field is increasing
 josh kii kami nahin
 Focus is on the pitch and eyes on the podium
 coach oltmens ko kamyaabi kaa fan maaloom he
 They take care of every nuance of the team and the player
 maidan par ek general kii bhoomika main hote hai to maidan ke baahar khilaadiyon ke khan-paan se lekar neend tak kaa puraa khyaal rakhte hai
 The players are beginning to understand why and what the coaches expect from them in the camp
 team hockey india ne beete ek saal main kai aisi kamyaabi hasil kii jisane hockey fans main badi ummid jagaai
 Defeating Pakistan in the final of the Incheon Asiad or defeating a team like Holland in the Champions Trophy in Bhubaneswar gave wings to the team's morale
 isi hausale ke sahare is team ne ajalan shah cap main australia jaisi team ko shikast de di
 Despite almost half a dozen players not fully fit in the World Hockey League semi-finals held in Belgium, the team stood fourth after Australia, Belgium and Britain
 lekin hockey ke adhikariyon ne is kamyaabi ko carat main badalane main der nahin lagaai
 It is another matter that players and coaches started talking about recovering from this loss as fast as possible
 1980 ke aakhri olympic medal ko hasil kiye 35 saal biit gaye hai
 Since then, the wait for the Olympic medal has been increasing
 shahrukh kii chak de parde par chaahe jitani hit rahi he bhartiya team ke liye sahi myne main chak de kehane kii chunauti barqaraar he
 The Olympic rate Olympics These teams keep increasing
 maujuuda team ek ummid jagaati he
 If the experts praise the merits of the team, then there is also a hint of deficiencies
 coach oltmens ne team hockey india kii penlti corner ko lekar bhi chintaa jataai he
 Indian drag flickers are considered great, but it is important to know how much they have compared to other countries of the world
 england ke eshle jackson, australia ke Chris Ciriello or germany ke philip jailer duniya ke maahir draig filkars maane jate hai
 The team as strong as drag flickers
 
 
 wo team utani hi kaamyaab! landan olympix se abtak bharat ne abtak top das tiimon ke kilaaf 67 maichon main 120 gol kiye or 176 gol khaaye! in 120 gol main 34 gol penlti corner ke zariye aaye
 India scored 24 penalty corners during the Champions Trophy and World Hockey League tournaments, in which the team scored just 9 goals
 jabaki bharat ke kilaaf inhen toornament main 41 penlti corner bane jinamein 14 gol hue
 Creating a penalty corner and turning it into a goal has proved to be a weak link for Team India in the recent tournament
 is ek kami ko dur kar bhartiya team bade kitaab jeet sakati he
 Experts say that the Indian team has power in the battery of short corner specialist but coaches Altmans are looking for other specialist besides Raghunath and Bob ie Rupinder
 gurjindar or jasjit jaise khilaadi achche vikalp ke taur par ubhar rahe hai
 Rupinder and VR Raghunath believe that the direction of their practice is right and they are expecting a lot from themselves and the team
 alag setapis, alag combination kii talash kii ja rahi he taaki bade maichon main iskaa bada faaydaa utaya ja sake
 Forward players are being told the tricks of penalty corner technique
 tippaniyan The team can definitely get the benefit of high altitude training at Shilaru at an altitude of 8000 ft above sea level
 lekin olympic ke podium kii oonchai tak pahunchane se pehle team kii chunautiyaan behad bad gai hai jiskaa jawaab puure hockey tantra ko dhundhna padegaa
 It can be said that no matter what the situation outside the field
 
 
 maidan par team kaa utsaah badhane laga he
 No lack of passion
 fokas pich par he or nazren podium par

 With this encouragement, this team defeated a team like Australia in Azlan Shah Cup
 belgium main hui world hockey lig semifinal main qareeb aadhe darjan khilaadiyon ke puri tarah se fit nahin hone ke baavjood ye team australia, belgium or britain ke baad chauthe number par rahi
 But hockey officials did not take long to convert this success into a carat
 ye or baat he ki khilaadi or coach utani hi tezi se is nuksaan se ubarne kii baat karne lage

 jis team ke draig flikars jitne damdaar

 sonu nigam ne ravivaar ko subah ajaan (maulaviyon kii ore se kii jane vaali prarthana) kaa video record kar twitor par daalaa he
 Looking at this video, it seems that it has been recorded in the early hours, it looks dark, but Ajan's voice is coming in it
 is video ke saath sonu nigam ne likhaa he, 'gudmorning india'

 yah bhi kaha ja rahaa he ki pichley dinon ek media santhaan ne daawa kiya tha ki sonu nigam ke ghar ke paas ajaan kii koi aawaaj nahin aati he

 dilli hai court ne kaha he ki apane naam kaa passport hasil karnaa or videsh yatra karnaa har naagarik kaa moulik adhikaar he
 The court has directed the Central Government to issue passport to the person who lost the passport thrice along with making such remarks
 nyaayamurti manmohan kii peeth ne videsh mantralay or sambandhit kshetreey karyaalay ko nirdesh diya ki yachikakarta e
 Passport should be issued again for development
 saath hi adaalat ne yachikakarta se kaha ki usne apane passport kaa dhyaan nahin rakhaa isliye use lokanayak jaiprakash narayan aspataal ko dharmarth 50 hajaar rupee dene chahie
 Justice Manmohan said, "after hearing the counsel of the petitioner and observing the file of the trial, this court believes that it is a fundamental right of every citizen to go abroad and obtain a passport in his name
 ' nyaayalay ne kaha ki maujuuda yachika or arji sweekaar kii jaati he or prativaadiyon ko yachikakarta ko phir se yaa vikalp ke rup main nayaa passport dene kaa nirdesh diya jaataa he
 The court said that the brother of the petitioner is also settled in Australia
 aisi sthiti main yachikarta ko passport nahin dene se uske moulik adhikaar kaa hanan hoga
 The passport was issued for the fourth time, according to the petitioner, he has lost his passport three times and was issued a passport by the regional office for the fourth time
 lekin usne ise kshatigrast haalat main lautaa diya
 The petitioner stated in the court that he had neither intentionally lost nor damaged the passport and had traveled peacefully to some countries for a short period

 kyonki aapkaa depressant main rahanaa aapke bachche ke liye khatarnaak sabit ho saktaa he

 yah study uniwarsity of landan ke shodhakartaaon dwaara kii gai he
 The lead author of this study, 'gemma Lewis', has said that there is a belief in society that the most negative effect on children is due to their mother's wrong behavior
 lekin hakeekat bilkul alag he
 He said that being in the father's depression has as much negative impact on the brains of children
 jitna unki maa ke depressant main hone ke kaaran hota he
 He has also told that due to both mother and father being in depression, the brain of children has an equally bad effect

 This study has been published in the Journal of Psychiatry
